global_colors_info="{}"]<h2>Wiluna Church</span></h2>
<span></span>

Discover a welcoming spiritual haven at Wiluna Seventh-day Adventist Church in Western Australia, Australia. Our church invites individuals and families to join us in worship, fellowship, and service. Engage in uplifting Sabbath worship services, enlightening Bible study groups, and meaningful community outreach initiatives. Whether you're exploring faith or seeking a supportive community, you'll find a place of belonging at Wiluna Seventh-day Adventist Church. Embrace the journey of faith with us as we seek to follow Christ's teachings and share His love with others. Visit Wiluna Seventh-day Adventist Church and become part of a caring Christian family dedicated to serving God and our community.
